	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	OutputLine(NULL, "………可哀想だよね…………………。」",
		   NULL, " awful............\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　頬を熱いものがぼろりと流れ落ちる＠.........俺の涙だった￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　頬を熱いものがぼろりと流れ落ちる。",
		   NULL, "Something hot burned down my cheeks.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "………俺の涙だった。",
		   NULL, " ......They were my tears.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//　俺はそれを乱暴に拭う＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　俺はそれを乱暴に拭う。",
		   NULL, "I fiercely wiped them away.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　......魅音に捧げられる最後の時間に、涙なんか絶対に見せたくなかったから＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　……魅音に捧げられる最後の時間に、涙なんか絶対に見せたくなかったから。",
		   NULL, "...This was the last of my time I could offer to Mion, so I absolutely didn't want to let her see my tears during it.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　もう魅音は玄関の外で待っていた............￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　もう魅音は玄関の外で待っていた…………。",
		   NULL, "Mion was already waiting outside the front door.........", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//if %kaisou_mode = 1 goto *kaisou_mode
	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(5, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene("black", 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

}
